==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// failure case
package xxx;
public class Foo {
    public void bar() {
        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar";
        x += "baz";
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 2

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().getParent().children(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();

            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightOperand instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                ASTStringLiteral stringLiteral = (ASTStringLiteral) rightOperand;

                if (variableAccess.getText().equals("x") && stringLiteral.isStringLiteral()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

5. Count the number of `+=` operations on string variables.
6. Check whether the count of `+=` operations on string variables is greater than 1.
7. Check whether a `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is explicitly used for string concatenation.

If the count of `+=` operations on string variables is greater than 1 and no explicit `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is used, then this test case violates the rule. 

In this test case:
- There are two `+=` operations on the string variable `x`.
- No explicit `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is used.
- Therefore, this test case violates the rule twice.

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                    ASTExpressionStatement expressionStatement = (ASTExpressionStatement) node.getParent();
                    if (expressionStatement.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock) {
                        ASTBlock block = (ASTBlock) expressionStatement.getParent();
                        int count = block.children(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                                .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT)
                                .filter(expr -> {
                                    ASTVariableAccess va = expr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                                    return va != null && va.getType() != null && va.getType().isString();
                                })
                                .count();
                        if (count > 1) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();

            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightOperand instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                ASTStringLiteral stringLiteral = (ASTStringLiteral) rightOperand;

                if (variableAccess.getText().equals("x") && stringLiteral.isStringLiteral()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccesses.anyMatch(var -> var.getName().equals("x"))) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null) {
                String varName = varAccess.getName();
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(assign -> assign.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT)
                    .filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null)
                    .filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class).getName().equals(varName));

                if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null) {
                String variableName = variableAccess.getName();
                List<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().children(ASTAssignmentExpression.class).toList();
                int count = 0;
                for (ASTAssignmentExpression assignment : assignments) {
                    if (assignment.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL) {
                        ASTVariableAccess currentVariableAccess = assignment.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                        if (currentVariableAccess != null && currentVariableAccess.getName().equals(variableName)) {
                            count++;
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                if (!JavaRuleUtil.isStringBuilderCtorOrAppend(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                ASTBlock block = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlock.class);
                if (block != null) {
                    NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                            .filter(assign -> assign.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT)
                            .filter(assign -> {
                                ASTVariableAccess access = assign.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                                return access != null && access.getType() != null && access.getType().isString();
                            });

                    if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getName().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getSymbol().getName().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getText().equals("=")) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator().equals("+")) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGNMENT && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) node.getRightOperand();
            if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            result += i;
        }

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(rightOperand)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            if (rightOperand instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) rightOperand;
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(infixExpr)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}

public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);

    }

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass(String.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass(String.class)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 7
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 7

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && "description".equals(leftOperand.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 7
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && "logStatement".equals(leftOperand.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && "logStatement".equals(leftOperand.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in do-loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        int i = 0;
        do {
            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.ASSIGN) {
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(rightOperand)) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class).forEach(assignment -> {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assignment.getRightOperand())) {
                ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = assignment.getLeftOperand();
                if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                    if (varAccess.getReferencedSym().getName().equals("logStatement")) {
                        addViolation(data, assignment);
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (varAccess.getReferencedSym().getName().equals("logStatement")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }

        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");

}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.ASTVariableAccess;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols.JVariableSymbol;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols.JFieldSymbol;
public boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
    JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
    if (sym instanceof JFieldSymbol) {
        JFieldSymbol fieldSym = (JFieldSymbol) sym;
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) && isFieldStringType(varAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTFieldDeclaration.class))) {
                    if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isFieldStringType(ASTFieldDeclaration node) {
        return TypeTestUtil.isA(String.class, node.getTypeNode());
    }
}

        2. Check whether the operand is an accessed field.
        3. Check whether the accessed field is a string type.
        4. Get the right-hand side operand of the assignment expression.
        5. Check whether the right-hand side operand is a string concatenation expression.
        6. Check whether the concatenation expression is inside a loop.

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

```
// violation: concat to String field in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isRepeatedStringAssignment(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringAssignment(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent()
            .ancestors(ASTBlock.class)
            .first()
            .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
            .filter(expr -> expr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess)
            .filter(expr -> ((ASTVariableAccess) expr.getLeftOperand()).getReferencedSym().equals(varAccess.getReferencedSym()))
            .filter(expr -> JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr.getRightOperand()));

        return assignments.count() > 1;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isRepeatedStringAssignment(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringAssignment(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        return assignments.filter(assign -> {
            ASTExpression left = assign.getLeftOperand();
            return left instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) left).getReferencedSym().equals(varAccess.getReferencedSym());
        }).count() > 1;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isRepeatedStringAssignment(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringAssignment(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
        if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
            JVariableSymbol sym = varAccess.getReferencedSym();
            if (sym instanceof JLocalVariableSymbol) {
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent()
                    .ancestors(ASTBlock.class)
                    .first()
                    .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(assign -> {
                        ASTExpression assignLeft = assign.getLeftOperand();
                        return assignLeft instanceof ASTVariableAccess && 
                               ((ASTVariableAccess) assignLeft).getReferencedSym() == sym;
                    });
                return assignments.count() > 1;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isRepeatedStringAssignment(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringAssignment(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent()
            .ancestors(ASTBlock.class)
            .first()
            .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
            .filter(expr -> expr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess)
            .filter(expr -> ((ASTVariableAccess) expr.getLeftOperand()).getReferencedSym().equals(varAccess.getReferencedSym()))
            .filter(expr -> JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr.getRightOperand()));

        return assignments.count() > 1;
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }
}
```

This checker has passed this negative testcase:
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isRepeatedStringAssignment(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringAssignment(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        return assignments.filter(assign -> {
            ASTExpression left = assign.getLeftOperand();
            return left instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) left).getReferencedSym().equals(varAccess.getReferencedSym());
        }).count() > 1;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isVariableAccessLocal(varAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessLocal(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JLocalVariableSymbol;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableDeclarator) {
                ASTVariableDeclarator varDecl = (ASTVariableDeclarator) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableDeclaratorInLoop(varDecl)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isVariableDeclaratorInLoop(ASTVariableDeclarator node) {
        ASTVariableDeclaratorId varId = node.getVarId();
        NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> varAccesses = varId.getLocalScope().getEnclosingScope(ASTBlock.class)
                .descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class)
                .filter(access -> access.getReferencedSym() == varId.getSymbol());
        return varAccesses.anyMatch(access -> access.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null);
    }
}

import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isVariableAccessLocal(varAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessLocal(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JLocalVariableSymbol;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (isVariableAccessField(varAccess) || isVariableAccessLocal(varAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessField(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JFieldSymbol;
    }

    private boolean isVariableAccessLocal(ASTVariableAccess node) {
        JVariableSymbol sym = node.getReferencedSym();
        return sym instanceof JLocalVariableSymbol;
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;

                }
            }
        }

This checker has passed this negative testcase:
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}

```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }
